  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="feed-reshare-content__commentary">üö® Human Cloud's Market Map V2 is LIVE üö®

Download Market Map here: <a class="link" href="https://hubs.li/Q03D6cjr0?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://hubs.li/Q03D6cjr0</a> 

üîé What is Market Map? A global snapshot of the best flexible talent solutions, with flexible talent defined as gig, freelance, fractional, and increasingly AI Agent workforces.

Market Map V2 does three things:

1: It quantifies the top 20% of solutions using Human Cloud's proprietary global ranking algorithm. For over 10 years Human Cloud has been building the Knowledge Graph for the flexible talent industry. Market Map is a data visualization product built off Knowledge Graph. 

2. It organizes solutions into their core value prop so that companies can use a lego block approach to use the best solutions fit for their specific purpose. The future belongs to specialized talent solutions, and while there are now 2,000+ solutions and over 14 different segments, AI is enabling every company to have specialization at scale. 

3. It visually shows the impact of AI and automation on the workforce. All the way to left is fully automated AI Agent workforces. While all the way to the right is fractional, executive workforces.

Congratulations to all solutions included!
-----------------

A HUGE shoutout to everyone involved! 

It was really tough to keep this secret.</p>
